   function lightboxControl() {

	})
	// if no cookies set, load and display the ad
	if (document.cookie.indexOf('lightbox_ad=') == -1) {
		console.log('no cookie present');
		setTimeout(() => {
			($lightbox).classList.add(lightboxShownClass);
			var date_toexpire = new Date();
			var hours = 8;

			var expires_lightbox = "; expires=" + date_toexpire.toGMTString();

		}, 3000);
	}

      <!-- User Code -->
      <script>
       window.onscroll = throttle(hideStickyAd,100);

function hideStickyAd(){
  var footer_div = document.getElementsByClassName("taboola-wrap")[0];
  var ad_div = document.getElementsByClassName("sticky-target")[1];
  var footer_pos = 0, ad_div_pos = 0;
  if(footer_div)
    footer_pos = footer_div.getBoundingClientRect().top;
  
  if(ad_div_pos)
    ad_div_pos = ad_div.getBoundingClientRect().top;

if(ad_div) {
  if(ad_div_pos>=footer_pos){
     ad_div.style.display = "none"; 
  } else {
     ad_div.style.display = "block"; 
  }
}
}

function throttle(callback, limit) {
    var wait = false;                  
    return function () {               
        if (!wait) {                  
            callback.call();           
            wait = true;              
            setTimeout(function () {   
                wait = false;          
            }, limit);
        }
    }
}
      </script>
      <!-- End User Code -->

function getParameterByName(name, url) {
    if (!url) url = window.location.href;
    name = name.replace(/[\[\]]/g, '\\$&');
    var regex = new RegExp('[?&]' + name + '(=([^&#]*)|&|#|$)'),
        results = regex.exec(url);
    if (!results) return null;
    if (!results[2]) return '';
    return decodeURIComponent(results[2].replace(/\+/g, ' '));
  }
